35 (655)
As╠Бvins
┼Ъy─Бv─Б┼Ыva ─Аtreya
24 verses: pariс╣гс╣н─Бjjyotis, except paс╣Еkti 22, 24 and mah─Бbr╠еhat─л 24, arranged in trcas. ╠е
The Anukramaс╣З─лтАЩs attribution of this hymn to ┼Ъy─Бv─Б┼Ыva is supported by his self-refer ence in verses 19тАУ21 and his reference to his ancestor Atri in verse 19, but the virtuos ity so characteristic of ┼Ъy─Бv─Б┼ЫvaтАЩs Marut hymns in Maс╣Зс╕Нala V is not on display here. This long hymn may be one of the most repetitive in the R╠еgveda. In the first twenty one verses the c-p─Бda is identical, and the tr╠еcas making up the hymn all have refrains encompassing at least the second half-verse (p─Бdas cd: vss. 1тАУ3; p─Бdas cde: vss. 22тАУ24) and usually the second (b) p─Бda as well (bcd: vss. 4тАУ6, 7тАУ9, 10тАУ12, 13тАУ15, 16тАУ18, 19тАУ21). This leaves the first (a) p─Бda as the only locus of variation in each tr╠еca, and even that variation is patterned and under strict control. Moreover, the contents and phraseology of the individual tr╠еcas do not differ significantly one from anotherтАФurg ing the A┼Ыvins to come to the sacrifice with numerous other gods and to partake of our offerings while providing us with gifts and aid in return. The repetitive structure has an incantatory effect, but it does not challenge the decoding skills of the audience.
The most interesting tr╠еca consists of verses 16тАУ18. As a number of others have pointed out, these three verses, asking the A┼Ыvins to тАЬquickenтАЭ or тАЬanimateтАЭ various things for us, are appropriate to the three varс╣Зas in turn: verse 16 to the brahmin, 17 to the kс╣гatriya, and 18 to the vai┼Ыya. In fact, verse 16 begins with the word bra╠Бhma, while 17 begins with kс╣гatra╠Бm. In 16 we ask for the A┼ЫvinsтАЩ aid for ritual and priestly elements, in 17 for elements related to kingly and martial power, and in 18 for our livestock and people. As is well known, the varс╣Зa system is not a prominent feature of the R╠еgveda and may well only be taking shape in this period, but this small collec tion of ┼Ъy─Бv─Б┼Ыva hymns displays it clearlyтАФnot only in this tr╠еca, but in the next two twinned hymns (36 and 37) with their reference to bra╠Бhman and kс╣гatra╠Б respectively.

+Jamison Brereton Notes

A┼Ыvins See the published introduction. for the pattern of repetitions in this very repetitious hymn.

The c p─Бda of every vs. save for the last three (22-24), тАЬin concert with Dawn and the SunтАЭ (saj├│с╣гas─Б uс╣г├бs─Б s┼л╠Бryeс╣Зa ca), of course refers to the A┼ЫvinsтАЩ participation in the dawn sacrifice.

тАЬAssociated with Agni, with Indra, with Varuс╣Зa, with Viс╣гс╣Зu, with the ─Аdityas, the Rudras, and theVasus, and united with the dawn and with S┼лrya, drink, A┼Ыvins, the Soma.тАЭ

+Jamison Brereton

With Agni, Indra, Varuс╣Зa, and Viс╣гс╣Зu, with the ─Аdityas, the Rudras, and the Vasus,
in concert with Dawn and the Sun, drink the soma, o A┼Ыvins.

+Griffith

WITH Agni and with Indra, Visnu. Varuna, with the Adityas, Rudras, Vasus, closely leagued;
Accordant, of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, O Asvins, drink the Soma juice.

+Geldner

+Grassmann

Mit Agni, Indra, Vischnu und mit Varuna, mit den Aditja’s, Rudra’s, Vasu’s im Verein, Mit Morgenroth und Sonne in Gemeinschaft trinkt, o Ritter ihr, den Somatrunk.

тАЬPowerful (A┼Ыvins), associated with all intelligences, with all beings, with heaven, with earth, with themountains, united with the dawn and with the S┼лrya, drink, A┼Ыvins, the Soma.тАЭ

+Griffith

Accordant. of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, O Asvins, drink the Soma juice.

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬBe gratified by the sacrifice; hear my invocation; recognize, deities, all the offerings in this ceremony;united with the dawn and with S┼лrya, bring us A┼Ыvins, food.тАЭ

+Jamison Brereton

Enjoy the sacrifice; take heed of my call. тАУ Come down here to all our pressings, o gods.
In concert with Dawn and the Sun, convey refreshment to us, o A┼Ыvins.

+Griffith

Accept the sacrifice, attend to this my call: come nigh, O ye Twain Gods, to all libations here.
Accordant, of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, O Asvins, bring us strengthening food.

+Geldner

Habt Wohlgefallen am Opfer, achtet auf meinen Ruf, findet euch, beide G├╢tter, bei allen Trinkopfern hier ein, eintr├дchtig mit Usas und Surya bringt uns Labsal, o Asvin!

+Grassmann

Geniesst das Opfer, achtet recht auf meinen Ruf; zu allen Spenden kommt, o G├╢tter hier herab, Und mit der Sonn’ und Morgenr├╢the im Verein, o Ritter, fahrt uns Labung zu.

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬYou hasten like two falcons to the offerer of the libation, you alight upon the effused Soma as twobuffaloes (hasten to water), united with the dawn and with S┼лrya, come, A┼Ыvins, by the triple path.тАЭ

+Jamison Brereton

Like falcons you fly to the distribution of oblations. тАУ Like buffaloes (to water), you come down to the pressed soma.
In concert with Dawn and the Sun, drive your circuit three times, o A┼Ыvins.

+Griffith

Ye fly to our oblation like a pair of hawks; like buffaloes ye seek the Soma we have shed.
Accordant, of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, come thrice, O Asvins, to our home.

Wie Falken flieget ihr zur Opferausteilung, ihr findet euch, beide G├╢tter, bei allen Trinkopfern hier ein, eintr├дchtig mit Usas und Surya bringt uns Labsal, o Asvin.

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬConquer (A┼Ыvins), your foes; protect and praise (your worshipper), grant progeny, give wealth, andunited with the dawn and with S┼лrya, give us, A┼Ыvins, strength.тАЭ

+Jamison Brereton

Conquer and sing praise and offer help. тАУ Provide progeny and provide property.
In concert with Dawn and the Sun, provide nourishment for us, o A┼Ыvins.

+Jamison Brereton Notes

The distribution of caтАЩs in p─Бda a is somewhat puzzling or, perhaps, syncopated, with the 2nd ca following preverb+verb (pr├б stutaс╣Г ca), though the other two preverb/verb combinations in this tс╣Ыca place the ca in the expected position after the preverb (─Б╠Бca gachatam 10a and immediately following pr├б c─Бvatam 11a). This does not seem to be metri causa, or at least not in some obvious way.

+Griffith

Conquer your foes, protect us, praise your worshippers; bestow upon us progeny and affluence.
Accordant, of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, O Asvins, grant us vigolms strength.

+Geldner

Sieget und stimmet das Lob an und helfet weiter und bringet Kinder und bringet Reichtum, eintr├дchtig mit Usas und Surya, bringet uns Kraft, o Asvin!

+Grassmann

Erweist euch r├╝hmlich, sieget und besch├╝tzet uns, und schenket Kinder, schenket reiche Sch├дtze uns, Vereinigt mit der Sonne und dem Morgenroth, o Ritter, gebet Speise uns.

+Jamison Brereton Notes

Exactly what dh├бrmavant- is conveying here is unclear, but it is highly unlikely to be, with Geldner, тАЬvon Dharma [den Gesetz] тАж begleitet,тАЭ since тАШlawтАЩ is quite anachronistic for dh├бrma(n)-. I also do not think Renou is correct in seeing it as a proper noun, despite its appearance in a -vant-stem parallel to those containing godsтАЩ names.

Rather, the repetitive template of the tс╣Ыca imposes the -vant-stem here, on the abstract principle dh├бrman- generally associated with Mitra and Varuс╣Зa – here perhaps referring to their authority and its manifestation (their statute) by which they impose order on the world.

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬHumblers of the pride (of your enemies), accept the earnest praises of ┼Ъy─Бv─Б┼Ыva offering youlibations as if you were accepting oblations; and, united with the dawn and with S┼лrya, (drink), A┼Ыvins, (theSoma) prepared the previous day.тАЭ

+Jamison Brereton

Like gushes (of water), send gushing the good praise hymns of the presser ┼Ъy─Бv─Б┼Ыva, o you roused to exuberance.
тАУ In concert with Dawn and the Sun, o A┼Ыvins, (drink) the (soma) aged overnight.

+Griffith

Further like running streams Syavasva’s eulogies who presses out the Soma, ye who reel in joy.
Accordant, of one mind with Surya and with Dawn, drink juice, O Asvins, three days old.

тАУ Drive here, o A┼Ыvins; come here. Seeking help, I call to you: provide riches for the pious man.

+Griffith

Drive down your chariot hitherward drink ye the Soma’s savoury juice.
Approach, ye Asvins, come to us: I call you, eager for your aid. Grant treasures to the worshipper.

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬCome, leaders of rites, when the sacrifice, at which your adoration is cited, is commenced, to drink ofthe Soma offered by me; come, A┼Ыvins, come (here), desirous of protection, I invoke you; give precious riches tothe donor of the offering.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Offered by me: vivakс╣гaс╣Зasya is an epithet of the speaker, i.e., at the commencementadoration of me the offerer of libation; or, it is an epithet of the Soma, heaven-bestowing, svargapr─Бpaс╣Зa┼Ы─лla

+Jamison Brereton
